<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превозносить.html>превозноси́ть</a> (24398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voznosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превозносить.html>превозноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevoznosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">превознести́</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to extol, to praise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превозносить.html>превозноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небе́с</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevoznosítʹ</b> do nebés</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to extol/praise to the skies</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превосходный.html>превосхо́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevosxódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превосходный.html>превосхо́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevosxódno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>superbly, fine, great, admirably
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:превосходный.html>превосхо́дно</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja čúvstvuju sebjá <b>prevosxódno</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I feel <b>great</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превосходный.html>превосхо́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevosxódno</span>)

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣвратити сѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prěvratiti sę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet with native <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перевороти́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevorotítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn into, to change into</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тность</a> (26539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">превра́тный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevrátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevrátnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vicissitude, changeability (a change, especially in one's life or fortunes)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превращение.html>превраще́ние</a> (7053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратить.html>преврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превращение.html>превраще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevraščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превращение.html>превраще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превращение.html>превраще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превращение.html>превраще́ний</a></b>)

<ol><li>change, transformation, conversion, transmutation, metamorphosis</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пря.html>пре́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ще́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>

***превышать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a> (4641)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevýsitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevyšátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exceed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevyšátʹ</b> vlastʹ / polnomóčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to exceed one's authority</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevyšátʹ</b> skórostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to speed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пря.html>пре́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ша́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>пре-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-выш-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превышение.html>превыше́ние</a> (16748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevýsitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превышение.html>превыше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevyšénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превышение.html>превыше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превышение.html>превыше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превышение.html>превыше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exceeding, excess
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превышение.html>превыше́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́сти</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чий</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevyšénije</b> vlásti/polnomóčij</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">exceeding one's authority</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a> (10675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предавать.html>предава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give oneself up <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнев.html>гне́ву</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:страсть.html>страстя́м</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> gnévu (strastjám)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give oneself up (abandon oneself) to anger (passions)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́янию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> otčájaniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give way to despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порок.html>поро́кам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> porókam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to indulge in vices</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечта.html>мечта́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> mečtám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie; lapse into daydreams</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предавать.html>предава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
